2535:    <!-- Functions -->
2536:    <xsl:template name="createMoney">
2537:       <xsl:param name="Curr"/>
2538:       <xsl:param name="AltCurr"/>
2539:       <xsl:param name="isCreditMemo"/>
2540:       <xsl:param name="money"/>
2541:       <xsl:param name="altAmt"/>
2542:       <xsl:param name="isLineNegPriceAdjustment"/>
2543:       <xsl:variable name="mainMoney">
2544:          <xsl:choose>
2545:             <xsl:when test="string($money) != ''">
2546:                <xsl:value-of select="$money"/>
2547:             </xsl:when>
2548:             <xsl:otherwise>0.00</xsl:otherwise>
2549:          </xsl:choose>
2550:       </xsl:variable>
2551:       <xsl:element name="Money">
2552:          <xsl:attribute name="currency">
2553:             <xsl:value-of select="$Curr"/>
2554:          </xsl:attribute>
2555:          <xsl:if test="$AltCurr != '' and $altAmt != ''">
2556:             <xsl:attribute name="alternateCurrency">
2557:                <xsl:value-of select="$AltCurr"/>
2558:             </xsl:attribute>
2559:             <xsl:attribute name="alternateAmount">
2560:                <xsl:choose>
2561:                   <xsl:when test="$isCreditMemo = 'yes'">
2562:                      <xsl:value-of select="concat('-', replace(string($altAmt), '-', ''))"/>
2563:                   </xsl:when>
2564:                   <xsl:otherwise>
2565:                      <xsl:value-of select="$altAmt"/>
2566:                   </xsl:otherwise>
2567:                </xsl:choose>
2568:             </xsl:attribute>
2569:          </xsl:if>
2570:          <xsl:choose>
2571:             <xsl:when test="$isLineNegPriceAdjustment = 'yes'">
2572:                <xsl:value-of select="concat('-', replace(string($mainMoney), '-', ''))"/>
2573:             </xsl:when>
2574:             <xsl:when test="$isLineNegPriceAdjustment = 'no'">
2575:                <xsl:value-of select="$mainMoney"/>
2576:             </xsl:when>
2577:             <xsl:when test="$isCreditMemo = 'yes'">
2578:                <xsl:value-of select="concat('-', replace(string($mainMoney), '-', ''))"/>
2579:             </xsl:when>
2580:             <xsl:otherwise>
2581:                <xsl:value-of select="$mainMoney"/>
2582:             </xsl:otherwise>
2583:          </xsl:choose>
2584:       </xsl:element>
2585:    </xsl:template>

4735:       <xsl:param name="Date"/>
4736:       <xsl:param name="Time"/>
4737:       <xsl:param name="TimeCode"/>
4738:       <xsl:variable name="timeZone">

4740:             <xsl:when test="$Lookup/Lookups/TimeZones/TimeZone[X12Code = $TimeCode]/CXMLCode != ''">
4741:                <xsl:value-of
4742:                   select="replace(replace($Lookup/Lookups/TimeZones/TimeZone[X12Code = $TimeCode]/CXMLCode, 'P', '+'), 'M', '-')"
4743:                />
4744:             </xsl:when>
4745:          </xsl:choose>
4746:       </xsl:variable>
4747:       <xsl:variable name="tempDate">
4748:          <xsl:value-of
4749:             select="concat(substring($Date, 1, 4), '-', substring($Date, 5, 2), '-', substring($Date, 7, 2))"
4750:          />
4751:       </xsl:variable>
4752:       <xsl:variable name="tempTime">
4753:          <xsl:choose>
4754:             <xsl:when test="$Time != '' and string-length($Time) = 6">
4755:                <xsl:value-of
4756:                   select="concat('T', substring($Time, 1, 2), ':', substring($Time, 3, 2), ':', substring($Time, 5, 2))"
4757:                />
4758:             </xsl:when>
4759:             <xsl:when test="$Time != '' and string-length($Time) = 4">
4760:                <xsl:value-of
4761:                   select="concat('T', substring($Time, 1, 2), ':', substring($Time, 3, 2))"/>
4762:             </xsl:when>
4763:          </xsl:choose>
4764:       </xsl:variable>
4765:       <xsl:choose>
4766:          <xsl:when test="$tempTime = ''">
4767:             <xsl:value-of select="''"/>
4768:          </xsl:when>
4769:          <xsl:otherwise>
4770:             <xsl:value-of select="concat($tempDate, $tempTime, $timeZone)"/>
4771:          </xsl:otherwise>
4772:       </xsl:choose>

002: <xsl:stylesheet xmlns:xsl="http://www.w3.org/1999/XSL/Transform" xmlns:xs="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:hci="http://sap.com/it/" exclude-result-prefixes="#all" version="2.0">
003:   <xsl:template name="convertToAribaDate">
004:     <xsl:param name="Date"/>
005:     <xsl:param name="Time"/>
006:     <xsl:param name="TimeCode"/>
007:     <xsl:variable name="timeZone">
008:       <xsl:choose>
009:         <xsl:when test="$Lookup/Lookups/TimeZones/TimeZone[X12Code = $TimeCode]/CXMLCode != ''">
010:           <xsl:value-of
011:             select="replace(replace($Lookup/Lookups/TimeZones/TimeZone[X12Code = $TimeCode]/CXMLCode, 'P', '+'), 'M', '-')"
012:           />
013:         </xsl:when>
014:         <xsl:otherwise>+00:00</xsl:otherwise>
015:       </xsl:choose>
016:     </xsl:variable>
017:     <xsl:variable name="temDate">
018:       <xsl:value-of
019:         select="concat(substring($Date, 1, 4), '-', substring($Date, 5, 2), '-', substring($Date, 7, 2))"
020:       />
021:     </xsl:variable>
022:     <xsl:variable name="tempTime">
023:       <xsl:choose>
024:         <xsl:when test="$Time != '' and string-length($Time) = 6">
025:           <xsl:value-of
026:             select="concat('T', substring($Time, 1, 2), ':', substring($Time, 3, 2), ':', substring($Time, 5, 2))"
027:           />
028:         </xsl:when>
029:         <xsl:when test="$Time != '' and string-length($Time) = 4">
030:           <xsl:value-of
031:             select="concat('T', substring($Time, 1, 2), ':', substring($Time, 3, 2), ':00')"/>
032:         </xsl:when>
033:         <xsl:otherwise>T12:00:00</xsl:otherwise>
034:       </xsl:choose>
035:     </xsl:variable>
036:     <xsl:value-of select="concat($temDate, $tempTime, $timeZone)"/>
037:   </xsl:template>
